    <component is="script" >        $(function() {
            $('.daterange').daterangepicker({
                'linkedCalendars': false,
                'showCustomRangeLabel': false,
                                                'opens': 'center',
                'drops': 'auto',
                'locale': { 'cancelLabel': 'Clear' },
            }, function (start, end, label) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val(start.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val(end.format('YYYY-MM-DD'));
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            }).on('cancel.daterangepicker', function(ev, picker) {
                let container = $('#game-logs');
                $('input[name="from"]', container).val('');
                $('input[name="to"]', container).val('');
                changeGameLogsFilter();
            });

            $('.daterange-opener').click(function() {
                $('.daterange').click();
            });
        });
    </component>                    </div>

                            <div class="SectionTitle"> Player Biography and Trivia </div>
                            <div class="pera">
                                                                                                            <p> Drafted <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/draft/khl-draft/2009">2009, 1 #8 overall by SKA St. Petersburg</a> in the KHL Draft </p>
                                                                    
                                
                                
                                                                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/2468/hpk-u20"> HPK U20 </a> </p>
                                                                            <p> Cult/Star player for <a href="https://www.eliteprospects.com/team/47/tappara"> Tappara </a> </p>
                                                                    
                                                                    <p><b>Career transactions</b><br>
- 2010-09-27 • Loaned to Tappara<br>
- 2010-05-11 • Signed to a three-year entry-level contract by the San Jose Sharks<br>
- 2009-03-12 • Signed to a two-year contract extension by Tappara
</p>
